   dolāyantre sāranāle tryahaṃ laghvagninā pacet /	dolAyantre sa AranAle tri aham laGu agninA pacet /

   ajīrṇaṃ cetpacedyantre kacchapākhye viḍānvitam /	ajIrNam ced pacet yantre kacCapa AKye vixa anvitam /

   ṭaṅkaṇaṃ śvetakācaṃ ca dattvā pṛṣṭhe nirudhya ca /	waFkaNam Sveta kAcam ca dattvA pRzWe niruDya ca /
   khadirāṅgārayogena dhamed yāvad drutaṃ bhavet // Rrā_2,3.15 //	Kadira aFgAra yogena Damet yAvat drutam Bavet // RrA_2,3.15 //
   tatastaṃ viḍaliptāyāṃ mūṣāyāṃ ca niveśayet /	tatas tam vixa liptAyAm mUzAyAm ca niveSayet /
   tattulyaṃ dāpayetsvarṇaṃ jayettaṃ dhaman dhaman // Rrā_2,3.16 //	tad tulyam dApayet svarNam jayet tam Daman Daman // RrA_2,3.16 //

   tasya vaktre gavāṃ kṣīraṃ stokaṃ stokaṃ niṣecayet /	tasya vaktre gavAm kzIram stokam stokam nizecayet /
   prabuddhe kṣīramannaṃ syādbhojane paramaṃ hitam // Rrā_2,3.74 //	prabudDe kzIram annam syAt Bojane paramam hitam // RrA_2,3.74 //

   jāyante padmarāgāṇi divyatejomayāni ca // Rrā_3,19.6 //	jAyante padmarAgANi divya tejaH mayAni ca // RrA_3,19.6 //
   {indranīlakaraṇam}	{indranIla karaNam}
   nīlīcūrṇaṃ palaikaṃ tu pūrvakūpyāṃ tu taddravam /	nIlI cUrNam pala ekam tu pUrva kUpyAm tu tad dravam /
   taddravaṃ dvipalaṃ cūrṇe kṣiptvā sarvaṃ vilolayet // Rrā_3,19.7 //	tad dravam dvi palam cUrNe kziptvA sarvam vilolayet // RrA_3,19.7 //
   kṣiptvā varṣotpalāṃstena pūrvatailagatānpacet /	kziptvA varza utpalAn= tena pUrva tEla gatAn pacet /
   indranīlāni tānyeva jāyante nātra saṃśayaḥ // Rrā_3,19.8 //	indranIlAni tAni eva jAyante na atra saMSayaH // RrA_3,19.8 //
   {marakatamaṇikaraṇam}	{marakata maNi karaNam}

   kācakūpyāṃ sthitairdrāvaiḥ sarvametat sulolayet // Rrā_3,19.9 //	kAca kUpyAm sTitEH drAvEH sarvam etat sulolayet // RrA_3,19.9 //
   varṣotpalāṃstu tenaiva siktvā pacyācca pūrvavat /	varza utpalAn= tu tena eva siktvA pacyAt ca pUrvavat /
   sarve marakatāstena samīcīnā bhavanti vai // Rrā_3,19.10 //	sarve marakatAH tena samIcInAH Bavanti vE // RrA_3,19.10 //
   {gomedamaṇikaraṇam}	{gomeda maNi karaNam}

   gomedāni tu tānyeva pravartante na saṃśayaḥ // Rrā_3,19.12 //	gomedAni tu tAni eva pravartante na saMSayaH // RrA_3,19.12 //
   {puṣparāgakaraṇam}	{puzparAga karaNam}

   tanmadhye cāṣṭamāṃśaṃ tu kṣipenmatsyotthakajjalam // Rrā_3,19.13 //	tad maDye ca azwama aMSam tu kzipet matsya utTa kajjalam // RrA_3,19.13 //
   tatsarvaṃ pācayedyāmam avatārya surakṣayet /	tat sarvam pAcayet yAmam avatArya surakzayet /

   bhavanti puṣparāgāste yathā khanyutthitāni ca // Rrā_3,19.14 //	Bavanti puzparAgAH te yaTA KanI utTitAni ca // RrA_3,19.14 //
   {nīlamāṇikyakaraṇam}	{nIla mANikya karaNam}

   {muktākaraṇam (2)}	{muktA karaNam (2)}

   {pravālakaraṇam (1)}	{pravAla karaNam (1)}

   {hiṅgukaraṇam (1)}	{hiFgu karaNam (1)}

   {hiṅgukaraṇam (2)}	{hiFgu karaNam (2)}
